different_country_flags_category = {
	
	### Custom ###
	#BRM
	BRM_reset_flag = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}
		allowed = { original_tag = BRM}
		visible = {
			original_tag = BRM
			has_elections = yes
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = BRM
				has_cosmetic_tag = BRM_Burma
				has_cosmetic_tag = BRM_Myanmar_federation
				has_cosmetic_tag = BRM_Burma_federation
				AND = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = {tag = BRM}
						has_cosmetic_tag = BRM_REB
						has_cosmetic_tag = BRM_REB_S
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision BRM_reset_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = BRM
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

	BRM_Autocracy_flag = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}
		allowed = { original_tag = BRM}
		visible = {
			original_tag = BRM
			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
			}
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = BRM_AUTH
				AND = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
						AND = {
							NOT = {tag = BRM}
							BRM = {
								OR = {
									has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
									has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
									has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision BRM_Autocracy_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = BRM_AUTH
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

	BRM_Special_flag = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation

		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}

		visible = {
			original_tag = BRM

			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
					}
					OR = {
						has_civil_war = no
						AND = {
							has_civil_war = yes
							tag = BRM
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag

	CAR_reset_flag = {

		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}
		allowed = { 
			OR = {
				original_tag = CAR
				original_tag = BAL
				original_tag = SEL
			}
		}
		visible = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = CAR
				AND = {
					original_tag = BAL
					NOT = {
						country_exists = CAR
						country_exists = SEL
					}
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = SEL
					NOT = {
						country_exists = CAR
						country_exists = BAL
					}
				}
			}
			has_elections = yes
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = CAR
				AND = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							tag = CAR
							tag = SEL
							tag = BAL
						}
						has_cosmetic_tag = CAR_REB
						has_cosmetic_tag = CAR_REB_S
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision CAR_reset_flag"

			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}

								has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
								AND = {
									NOT = {
										tag = SUD
									}
									SUD = {
										OR = {
											has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
											has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
											has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = SRF
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							has_civil_war = yes
							OR = {
								has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
								AND = {
									NOT = {
										tag = SRF
									}
									SRF = {
										OR = {
											has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
											has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
											has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						country_exists = SUD
					}
				}
			}
			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
			}
			NOT = {has_cosmetic_tag = SUD_AUTH}

		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}
		allowed = { original_tag = COL}
		visible = {
			original_tag = COL
			has_elections = yes
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = COL
				AND = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = {tag = COL}
						has_cosmetic_tag = COL_REB
						has_cosmetic_tag = COL_REB_S
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision COL_reset_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = COL
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

	COL_Autocracy_flag = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}
		allowed = { original_tag = COL}
		visible = {
			original_tag = COL
			has_elections = no
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
			}
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = COL_AUTH
				AND = {
					has_civil_war = yes
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy
						AND = {
							NOT = {tag = COL}
							COL = {
								OR = {
									has_country_leader_with_trait = western_Western_Autocracy
									has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Autocracy
									has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Autocracy
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision COL_Autocracy_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = COL_AUTH
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

	COL_Special_flag = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		cost = 0
		ai_will_do = { factor = 1}
		allowed = { original_tag = COL}
		visible = {
			original_tag = COL
			has_elections = no
			NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = COL_AUTH_S }
			OR = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = salafist_Kingdom
				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Monarchist
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_with_trait = emerging_Communist-State
						has_country_leader_with_trait = neutrality_Neutral_Communism
					}
					OR = {
						has_civil_war = no
						AND = {
							has_civil_war = yes
							tag = COL
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision COL_Special_flag"
			set_cosmetic_tag = COL_AUTH_S
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_change_flag
		}
	}

			COL = { has_cosmetic_tag = COL }

				has_cosmetic_tag = COL_REB
				tag = COL

				has_country_leader_with_trait = nationalist_Nat_Autocracy

		}
